EXCELLENT Service, Location... and GOOD FOOD: healthy, fresh, organic and tasty!!!! No SODAS! But the lemonade basil is so yummy! It's a place worth the drive from Irvine to Dana Point. The appetizer with the salmon... delicious! The different types of combination salad with a topping if steak or salmon... totally filling! The chicken dish ... sorry, can't remember (starts with a "p") ... flavor was divine, smoked edge ... just delicious! Sorry but neither my mom who ordered the appetizer or my brother who ordered the chicken plate and I with the spring salad and salmon have no left overs! That's how delicious and perfectly portioned the meals were. Yummy to the moon and back.<//Review>

Exceeded my expectations. Everything was so yummy here! And the eggs were cooked perfectly - both over hard & poached. And the coffee was fire. They have really good cashew milk and really tasty latte flavors. There's plenty of parking, but we came early and parked at the harbor. Overall waited about 20 minutes for seating outside on a beautiful day.</Text>

< Text>
Maison Cafe is a gem! The decor is warm and cozy and reminded me of a  cafe you would see in the back country of Italy. The menu is specifically selected using the best organic ingredients available by season.   My choice was the Turmeric Hummus Appetizer and Wine. My heart filled with joy when my bountiful and colorful plate of healthy goodness arrived to my table! The flavors were so delicious.  Owner Danielle's belief and vision is that we all deserve healthy, organic and delicious food - I can say she has perfected it.  She visits with her guest and when I met her briefly I could sense she is a very special soul leaving her own positive footprint on this earth one plate at a time.  When you are in the mood for a "Getaway" step inside Maison Cafe + Market.</Text>

<username>Theresa Aslin<//username><Time>1562744396448<//Time><Rating>5< /Rating>< Review>
My mom and I are always on the hunt for exquisite French restaurants. This one is unusual because its upscale and understated at the same time. The dress code is casual and the vide is industrial but country, too, and the food is marvelous.
Just wonderful. I had the Mushroom Tartine and my mom had the Duck Confit Tartine. Both were delicious and just perfectly light and filling. We also each had a basil lemonade which was fantastically refreshing. The parking here is a pain. The lot is tiny and people are going in and out to shop at the surf store next door. Nonetheless I would come back anytime.
The server was attentive.
My mom had taken me here for the croissants which are made fresh daily, but we were too late. Our server indicated they are usually gone by noon. We didn't get seated until 1pm. The wait was only about 20 minutes for a party of 2, and it was definitely worth it (I don't say that often).</Review>

This review is specifically geared towards the outstanding service provided by the team here at Greco's

We had a pizza party here for our daughter's birthday yesterday, and let me tell you, the staff here did EVERYTHING to make the experience an amazing one, and not once asked for anything in return (other than paying for our food/drinks of course).

I have really never had such stellar service like we had here yesterday.
